    1728            8 :     private assertObjectsEqual<T>(fullActual: T, fullExpected: T, msgPrefix = ""): void {
    1729          564 :         const recur = <U>(actual: U, expected: U, path: string) => {
    1730         1144 :             const fail = (msg: string) => {
    1731            0 :                 this.raiseError(`${msgPrefix} At ${path}: ${msg} ${displayExpectedAndActualString(stringify(fullExpected), stringify(fullActual))}`);

    1734         1144 :             if ((actual === undefined) !== (expected === undefined)) {
    1735            0 :                 fail(`Expected ${stringify(expected)}, got ${stringify(actual)}`);
    1736            0 :             }
    1737         1144 : 
    1738         1144 :             for (const key in actual) {
    1739        13628 :                 if (ts.hasProperty(actual as any, key)) {
    1740        13628 :                     const ak = actual[key], ek = expected[key];
    1741        13628 :                     if (typeof ak === "object" && typeof ek === "object") {
    1742          580 :                         recur(ak, ek, path ? path + "." + key : key);
    1743          580 :                     }
    1744        13048 :                     else if (ak !== ek) {
    1745            0 :                         fail(`Expected '${key}' to be '${stringify(ek)}', got '${stringify(ak)}'`);
    1746            0 :                     }
    1747        13628 :                 }
    1748        13628 :             }
    1749         1144 : 
    1750         1144 :             for (const key in expected) {
    1751        13345 :                 if (ts.hasProperty(expected as any, key)) {
    1752        13345 :                     if (!ts.hasProperty(actual as any, key)) {
    1753            0 :                         fail(`${msgPrefix}Missing property '${key}'`);
    1754            0 :                     }
    1755        13345 :                 }
    1756        13345 :             }

    1758          564 :

    4576            8 : function forEachTextChange(changes: readonly ts.TextChange[], cb: (change: ts.TextChange) => void): void {

    4580            8 :         const change = changes[i];

    4584            8 :             if (changes[j].span.start >= change.span.start) {
    4585            8 :                 changes[j].span.start += changeDelta;

    4591            8 : function updatePosition(position: number, editStart: number, editEnd: number, { length }: string): number {
